    <script type="text/template" id="header-content-nomatch">
      <div class="Header-wrapper l-container">
        <div class="Header-logoWrapper">

        <div class="Header-rightSection" role="navigation">
          <ul class="Header-barLinkWrapper--right">
            <li class="Header-barItem Header-barItem--right">
              <a class="Header-barLink Header-login white-bar-link" href="https://www.farmers.com/search/" data-ya-track="search">
                <span class="material-icons" translate="no">search</span>
                <span class="Header-linkText">
                  <span class="sr-only">Search</span>
                </span>
              </a>
            </li>
            <li class="Header-barItem Header-barItem--right">
              <a class="Header-barLink Header-login white-bar-link" href="https://www.farmers.com/login/" data-ya-track="login">

    <script>
      (function() {
      var contentHolder=document.createElement('div');
      var existingContentNodes=[];
      var replaceContent=function(target, html) {
          while (existingContentNodes.length > 0) {
              var child=existingContentNodes.pop();
              child.parentNode.removeChild(child);
          }
          contentHolder.innerHTML=html;
          while (contentHolder.childNodes.length > 0) {
              existingContentNodes.push(contentHolder.firstChild);
              target.parentNode.appendChild(contentHolder.firstChild);
          }
      }
      ;
      var loadContent=function() {
          var template=document.getElementById('header-content');
          replaceContent(template, template.innerHTML);
          window.dispatchEvent(new Event('header-mobile'));
      }
      ;
      var loadNonMatchingContent=function() {
          var template=document.getElementById('header-content-nomatch');
          replaceContent(template, template.innerHTML);
          window.dispatchEvent(new Event('header-desktop'));
      }
      ;
      var listener=function(query) {
          if (query.matches) {
              loadContent();
          }
          else {
              loadNonMatchingContent();
          }
      }
      ;
      if(window.matchMedia) {
          var mq=window.matchMedia('(max-width: 61.9375em)');
          mq.addListener(listener);
          if (mq.matches) {
              loadContent();
          }
          else {
              loadNonMatchingContent();
          }
      }
      else {
          loadContent();
      }
      }

      )();
    </script>
  </div>

<script>
    function getCurrentYear() {
        const currentDate = new Date();
        return currentDate.getFullYear();
    }

    $("c-copy-date").html(`&copy; ${getCurrentYear()}`);

    document
        .getElementById("js-ccpa-banner-close")
        .addEventListener("click", () => {
            hideBanner(), getSession() || setSession();
        }),
        getSession() || addBanner();

    function addBanner() {
        const i = document.getElementById("js-ccpa-banner"),
            c = document.getElementById("js-main-page-wrapper"),
            f = document.getElementById("js-footer-white");
        i.classList.remove("hidden"),
            f.classList.remove("banner-hidden"),
            c != null && c.classList.add("banner-open");
    }
    function hideBanner() {
        const i = document.getElementById("js-ccpa-banner"),
            c = document.getElementById("js-main-page-wrapper"),
            f = document.getElementById("js-footer-white");
        i.classList.add("hidden"),
            f.classList.add("banner-hidden"),
            c != null && c.classList.remove("banner-open");
    }

    function setSession() {
        return setCookie("sessionActive", "is-active", 1 / 48, "/");
    }
    function getSession() {
        return this.getCookie("sessionActive");
    }

    function setCookie(t, i, s, u, f) {
        let c = new Date();
        c.setTime(c.getTime() + s * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1e3);
        let l = `expires=${c.toUTCString()}`,
            d = t + "=" + encodeURIComponent(i) + "; " + l;
        return (
            u && (d += `; path=${u}`),
            f && (d += `; domain=${f}`),
            (document.cookie = d)
        );
    }

    function getCookie(t) {
        let i = t + "=",
            s = document.cookie.split(";");
        for (
            let u = 0, f = s.length, c = 0 <= f;
            c ? u < f : u > f;
            c ? u++ : u--
        ) {
            let l = s[u];
            for (; l.charAt(0) === " "; ) l = l.substring(1);
            if (l.indexOf(i) === 0)
                return decodeURIComponent(l.substring(i.length, l.length));
        }
        return !1;
    }
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("input[name=phone1]").on("focus", function () {
            $(this).parents(".f-form-control").removeClass("f-focus");
        });
        $("input[name=phone1]").on("blur", function () {
            if ($(this).val()) {
                return;
            }
            $(this).parents(".f-form-control").addClass("f-focus");
        });
    });

<script>
    const oForm = {
        init: function (formId, resetForm) {
            const parsleyForm = $(`#${formId}`)
                .parsley()
                .on("form:success", function (e) {
                    // processForm(formId);
                    grecaptcha.execute();
                    e.submitEvent.preventDefault();
                    return false;
                });

            $(".open-the-modal").click(function () {
                $("html").addClass("open-modal");
                $(`#${$(this).attr("data-modal")}`).fadeIn();
            });

            $(".f-modal-close").click(function () {
                $("html").removeClass("open-modal");
                $(this).parents(".f-modal").fadeOut();
                parsleyForm.reset();
                resetForm();
            });

            $(".f-modal").click(function () {
                $("html").removeClass("open-modal");
                $(this).fadeOut();
                parsleyForm.reset();
                resetForm();
            });

            $(".f-modal-box").click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
            });
        },
    };
</script>

<script id="js-date-data-MONDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-TUESDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-WEDNESDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-THURSDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-FRIDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-SATURDAY" type="text/data"></script>
<script id="js-date-data-SUNDAY" type="text/data"></script>

<script>
    class n {
        constructor() {
            (this.stateSelectEl = document.querySelector(".js-time-picker")),
                (this.calendarEl = document.querySelector(
                    ".js-date-calendarWrapper"
                )),
                (this.mondayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-MONDAY"
                )),
                (this.tuesdayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-TUESDAY"
                )),
                (this.wednesdayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-WEDNESDAY"
                )),
                (this.thursdayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-THURSDAY"
                )),
                (this.fridayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-FRIDAY"
                )),
                (this.saturdayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-SATURDAY"
                )),
                (this.sundayHoursData = document.getElementById(
                    "js-date-data-SUNDAY"
                ));

            this.specialHours = this.getSpecialHours();
        }
        getSpecialHours() {
            const _specialHoursTxt = "";
            if (!_specialHoursTxt) {
                return null;
            }

            let _specialHoursObj = _specialHoursTxt.split(",");
            let _specialHours = {};

            $.each(_specialHoursObj, function (key, val) {
                var _newVal = val.split(" ");

                _specialHours[_newVal[0]] = _newVal[1]
                    .replace(/:/g, "")
                    .split("-");
            });

            return _specialHours;
        }
        setupCalendar(i) {
            const r = {
                    input: document.querySelector(".js-date"),
                    calendarContainer: document.querySelector(
                        ".js-date-calendarWrapper"
                    ),
                },
                a = new Date();
            a.setDate(a.getDate() + 1);
            const o = new Pikaday({
                bound: !0,
                field: r.input,
                container: r.calendarContainer,
                minDate: a,
                theme: "appt",
                format: "MM/DD/YY",
                onSelect(l) {
                    r.input.parentNode.classList.add("js-selected-date"),
                    i.updateHours(l);
                    $(r.input).parsley().validate();
                },
                disableDayFn(l) {
                    const specialHour = i.getSpecialHour(l);

                    if (specialHour) {
                        if (specialHour[0] == "Closed") {
                            return true;
                        }
                    } else {
                        const d = i.dateNumberToData(l.getDay());
                        return !(d.start !== null && d.end !== null);
                    }
                },
            });
        }
        getSpecialHour(date) {
            const month = ("0" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2); //add leading zero to single digits
            const day = ("0" + date.getDate()).slice(-2); //add leading zero to single digits
            const dateString = `${month}-${day}-${date.getFullYear()}`;

            if (this.specialHours && dateString in this.specialHours) {
                return this.specialHours[dateString];
            }

            return null;
        }
        specialHourData(date) {
            const specialHour = this.getSpecialHour(date);

            if (specialHour) {
                return {
                    start: this.formatBhoTime(
                        +specialHour[0].split(":").join("")
                    ),
                    end: this.formatBhoTime(
                        +specialHour[1].split(":").join("")
                    ),
                };
            }

            return null;
        }
        setupInterests() {
            const t = document.querySelectorAll(".f-interest-list li");
            for (const i of t) {
                const s = i.querySelector(".f-interest-list li input");
                s &&
                    s.addEventListener("click", () => {
                        s.checked = !s.checked;
                    }),
                    i.addEventListener("click", () => {
                        i.classList.toggle("f-selected");
                        const { selected: u } = i.dataset;
                        u
                            ? i.dataset.selected == "false"
                                ? (i.dataset.selected = !0)
                                : (i.dataset.selected = !1)
                            : (i.dataset.selected = !0),
                            (s.checked = !s.checked);
                    });
            }
        }
        updateHours(i) {
            const r = i.getDay(),
                a = this.specialHourData(i)
                    ? this.specialHourData(i)
                    : this.dateNumberToData(r);
            let o = 0,
                l = 2400;
            for (
                a.start && (o = a.start),
                    a.end && (l = a.end),
                    this.removeAllChildNodes(this.stateSelectEl);
                o < l;

            ) {
                const d = this.getTimeStamp(o, !1),
                    f = document.createElement("option");
                (f.innerHTML = d),
                    this.stateSelectEl.appendChild(f),
                    (o += 15),
                    o % 100 == 60 && (o += 40);
            }
        }
        dateNumberToData(i) {
            let r;
            switch (i) {
                case 0:
                    r = this.sundayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 1:
                    r = this.mondayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 2:
                    r = this.tuesdayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 3:
                    r = this.wednesdayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 4:
                    r = this.thursdayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 5:
                    r = this.fridayHoursData;
                    break;
                case 6:
                    r = this.saturdayHoursData;
                    break;
            }
            return JSON.parse(r.innerHTML);
        }
        getTimeStamp(i, r) {
            const a = Math.floor(i / 100),
                o = `00${i % 100}`;
            let l = "";
            return (
                r
                    ? (l = `${a}:${o.slice(-2)}`)
                    : ((l = `${a}:${o.slice(-2)} AM`),
                      a === 12 && (l = `12:${o.slice(-2)} PM`),
                      a >= 13 && (l = `${a - 12}:${o.slice(-2)} PM`),
                      a === 0 && (l = `12:${o.slice(-2)} AM`)),
                l
            );
        }
        removeAllChildNodes(i) {
            if (i) for (; i.firstChild; ) i.removeChild(i.firstChild);
        }
        setupDates(g) {
            const days = [
                "SUNDAY",
                "MONDAY",
                "TUESDAY",
                "WEDNESDAY",
                "THURSDAY",
                "FRIDAY",
                "SATURDAY",
            ];
            const bho = g.convertBhoToArray("[[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;]]");

            bho.forEach((item, index) => {
                let start = g.formatBhoTime(item[0]);
                let end = g.formatBhoTime(item[1]);
                document.getElementById(
                    `js-date-data-${days[index]}`
                ).innerHTML = `{"start": ${start}, "end": ${end}}`;
            });
        }
        convertBhoToArray(temp) {
            // temp = temp.replace(/&quot;/g, "");
            // temp = temp.replace(/01/g, "1");
            // temp = temp.replace(/02/g, "2");
            // temp = temp.replace(/03/g, "3");
            // temp = temp.replace(/04/g, "4");
            // temp = temp.replace(/05/g, "5");
            // temp = temp.replace(/06/g, "6");
            // temp = temp.replace(/07/g, "7");
            // temp = temp.replace(/08/g, "8");
            // temp = temp.replace(/09/g, "9");
            // temp = temp.replace(/0000/g, "1159");

            temp = temp.replace(/&quot;/g, "");
            temp = temp.replace(/0000/g, "1159");
            temp = temp.replace(/\b0+(\d+)\b/g, '$1');

            return JSON.parse(temp);
        }
        formatBhoTime(time) {
            let theTime = time;
            if (
                time === 9999 ||
                time == "9999" ||
                time === "closed" ||
                time === 8799 ||
                time === ""
            ) {
                theTime = "null";
            }
            return theTime;
        }
    }

    const g = new n();
    g.setupDates(g);
    g.setupCalendar(g);
    g.setupInterests();
</script>
<!-- end: scripts from live -->

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        function resetAppointmentForm() {
            $('#form-appointment').parent().find('.thank-you').hide();
            $('#form-appointment').show();

            $('input[name="firstName"]').val("");
            $('input[name="lastName"]').val("");
            $('input[name="email"]').val("");
            $('input[name="phone1"]').val("");
            $('input[name="date"]').val("");
            $("select[name='time']")
                .find("option")
                .remove()
                .end()
                .append('<option value="n/a">Select a time</option>')
                .val("n/a");
            $('input[name="isCustomer"][value="false"]').prop("checked", true);
            $("input:checkbox:checked").prop("checked", false);
            $(".f-selected").removeClass("f-selected");
        }

        oForm.init("form-appointment", resetAppointmentForm);
    });
</script>

            $("select[name='contactReason']").val("n/a");
        }

    });

<script type="text/javascript">
    function formatPhoneNumber(phoneNumberString) {
        var cleaned = ("" + phoneNumberString).replace(/\D/g, "");
        var match = cleaned.match(/^(1|)?(\d{3})(\d{3})(\d{4})$/);
        if (match) {
            // var intlCode = match[1] ? "+1 " : "";
            return ["(", match[2], ") ", match[3], "-", match[4]].join("");
        }
    
        return null;
    }

    const phones = document.querySelectorAll('.f-formatted-phone');
    phones.forEach(function(phone) {
        const formattedPhone = formatPhoneNumber(phone.innerHTML);
        phone.innerHTML = formattedPhone;
        phone.href = `tel:${formattedPhone}`;
    })
</script>

<script>
  window.addEventListener('load', setLocationData());

function setLocationData() {
  var _agentName = 'Nicholas Keton Martinez - 8008 Camp Bowie West Blvd ';
  var _agentState = 'TX';
  var _agentNumber = '35905M';

  var _agent = {
    "name": _agentName,
    "agent_state": _agentState,
    "agent_number": _agentNumber
  };

  setCookie('lastViewedAgent', JSON.stringify(_agent), 30, 'agents.farmers.com', '/');
}

// Function to set a cookie
function setCookie(name, value, days, domain, path) {
  if (getCookie(name) !== null) {
    deleteCookie(name, domain, path);
  }

  let expires = '';
  if (days) {
    const date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
  }
  document.cookie = name + '=' + value + expires + '; domain=' + domain + '; path=' + path;
}

// Function to get a cookie value
function getCookie(name) {
  const nameEQ = name + '=';
  const cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
  for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
    let cookie = cookies[i];
    while (cookie.charAt(0) === ' ') {
      cookie = cookie.substring(1, cookie.length);
    }
    if (cookie.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) {
      return decodeURIComponent(cookie.substring(nameEQ.length, cookie.length));
    }
  }
  return null;
}

// Function to delete a cookie
function deleteCookie(name, domain, path) {
  document.cookie = name + '=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; domain=' + domain + '; path=' + path;
}

  if (
    "Texas" == "Maine" ||
    "Texas" == "New Hampshire" ||

    "Texas" == "Kentucky" ||

  }

<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", (event) => {
    const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    if (searchParams.get('contact') == 'true') {
      setTimeout(() => {
        document.querySelector('button[data-modal="contact-modal"]').click()
      }, 1000)
    }

  });

  let allPhoneNeededToConvert = document.querySelectorAll(".phoneData");
  allPhoneNeededToConvert.forEach((item) => {
    let phone = convertPhone(item.getAttribute("data-value"));
    item.innerHTML = phone;
  });

  function convertPhone(phone) {
    if (phone && phone.includes("+1 ")) {
        let phoneData = phone.replace("+1 ", "").split("-");
        return `(${phoneData[0]}) ${phoneData[1]}-${phoneData[2]}`;
    } else {
        return phone;
    }
  }


</script>

				function convertTimestampToAMPM(timestamp) {
					const milliseconds = timestamp * 1000;
					const date = new Date(milliseconds);
					let hours = date.getHours();
					const minutes = ("0" + date.getMinutes()).slice(-2);
					const ampm = hours >= 12 ? "AM" : "PM";
					hours = hours % 12;
					hours = hours ? hours : 12;
					const formattedTime = `${hours}:${minutes} ${ampm}`;
					return formattedTime;
				}

	let allSpotlightContainerCheck = document.querySelectorAll(".ContentSpotlightItem-wrapper");
	if (allSpotlightContainerCheck.length > 0) {
		document.querySelector("#ask-me-about").style.display = "block";
	}

	if (window.location.hash) {
		let hash = window.location.hash;
		if (hash == "#reviews") {
			$("html, body").animate(
				{
					scrollTop: $("#reviews").offset().top - 215,
				},
				1000
			);
		}
	}

}

<script>

  // More modal function
  const oHTMLTag = $('html');
  const oMoreModal = $('#More-modal');
  const oMoreModalClose = $('#more-modal-close');
  const oContentMoreButton = $('#js-state-More');
  const oFoatingMoreButton = $('#InsuranceProducts--more');


  function modalCloseButon() {
    oMoreModalClose.on('click', function() {
      oMoreModal
        .removeClass('in')
        .css('display', 'none');
      oHTMLTag.css('overflow-y', 'initial');
    });
  }

  function moreButtonEvent(oButton) {
    oButton.on('click', function(){
      oMoreModal
        .addClass('in')
        .css('display', 'block');
      oHTMLTag.css('overflow-y', 'hidden');
    });
  }

  function moreModalInit() {
    moreButtonEvent(oContentMoreButton);
    moreButtonEvent(oFoatingMoreButton);
    modalCloseButon();
  }

  moreModalInit();

function insertAggregateRatingSchema(average, count, reviewItems)
{
   let structuredDataTextReview = "";
   structuredDataTextReview += '{';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "@context": "https://schema.org/",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "@type": "LocalBusiness",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "image": "https://p1.socds.net/llp/6095/photo_upload_65b0457716561-2024-01-23.jpg",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "name": "Nicholas Martinez",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "telephone": "+1 817-887-9043",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "address": {';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "@type": "PostalAddress",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "addressCountry": {';
   structuredDataTextReview += '         "@type": "Country",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '         "name": "US"';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      },';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "addressLocality": "Fort Worth",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "addressRegion": "TX",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "streetAddress": "8008 Camp Bowie West Blvd",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '      "postalCode": "76116"';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   },';
   structuredDataTextReview += '   "review": [';
   let reviewCtr = 0;
   $.each(reviewItems, function(item, review) {
      if (reviewCtr < reviewItems.length) {
         structuredDataTextReview += '{';
         structuredDataTextReview += '   "@type": "Review",';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "reviewRating": {';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "@type": "Rating",';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "worstRating": "1",';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "bestRating": "5",';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "ratingValue": "'+review.rating_value+'"';
         structuredDataTextReview += '   },';
         structuredDataTextReview += '   "author": {';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "@type": "Person",';
         structuredDataTextReview += '      "name": "'+review.author_name+'"';
         structuredDataTextReview += '   }';
         structuredDataTextReview += '}';
         structuredDataTextReview += (reviewCtr < reviewItems.length - 1) ? ',' : '';
         reviewCtr++;
      }
   });
   structuredDataTextReview += '    ],';
   structuredDataTextReview += '    "aggregateRating": {';
   structuredDataTextReview += '       "@type": "AggregateRating",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '       "ratingValue": "'+average+'",';
   structuredDataTextReview += '       "ratingCount": "'+count+'"';
   structuredDataTextReview += '    }';
   structuredDataTextReview += '}';

   var scriptStructuredDataReview = document.createElement('script');
   scriptStructuredDataReview.setAttribute('type', 'application/ld+json');
   scriptStructuredDataReview.textContent = structuredDataTextReview;
   document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(scriptStructuredDataReview);
}

  function processReviewsData(data) {
      if (data) {
          var _total = data.summary.items_total;
          var _avgRating = data.summary.rating_value;
          var _reviews = data.items;

          let _return = [];
          _return.total = _total;
          _return.average = _avgRating;
          _return.reviews = _reviews;

          return _return;

      } else {
          return [];
      }
  }

  function convertMonth(sMonth) {
    let currentMonth = sMonth;

    if (currentMonth === '01') {
      currentMonth = 'January';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '02') {
      currentMonth = 'February';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '03') {
      currentMonth = 'March';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '04') {
      currentMonth = 'April';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '05') {
      currentMonth = 'May';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '06') {
      currentMonth = 'June';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '07') {
      currentMonth = 'July';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '08') {
      currentMonth = 'August';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '09') {
      currentMonth = 'September';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '10') {
      currentMonth = 'October';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '11') {
      currentMonth = 'November';
    } else
    if (currentMonth === '12') {
      currentMonth = 'December';
    }

    return currentMonth;
  }

  function getPastDuration(dateString) {
    let reviewDate = dateString;
        reviewDate = reviewDate.split(' ');
        reviewDate = reviewDate[0];
        reviewDate = reviewDate.split('-');
    const reviewMonth = reviewDate[1];
    const reviewDay = reviewDate[2];
    const reviewYear = reviewDate[0];
    const convertedDate = convertMonth(reviewMonth) + ' ' + reviewDay + ', ' + reviewYear;

    return convertedDate;
  }

  function populateReviewsHtml(data, sClass) {
    if (data.reviews.length > 0) {

        let iLoopCount = 0;
        let _reviews = '<div class="reviewSlideItemWrap">';
        let reviewCtr = 0;
        
        function appendReviews(review, count) {
          let dateDuration = getPastDuration(review.date);

          let reviewAverage = review.rating_value;

          // 4.8, 4.9, 5.0 show 5 full stars
          if(Math.abs(5.0 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){ 
          //do nothing, show 5 stars
          }
          
          //4.3, 4.4, 4.5, 4.6, 4.7 will show the half star at the end
          if(Math.abs(4.5 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2) {
          reviewAverage = "4_5";   
          }

          //3.8, 3.9, 4.0, 4.1, 4.2 show one empty star at the end
          if (Math.abs(4.0 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2) { 
          reviewAverage = "4_0"; 
          }

          //3.3, 3.4, 3.5, 3.6, 3.7 show one empty star at the end and 1 half star before that
          if(Math.abs(3.5 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          reviewAverage = "3_5";
          }

          //2.8, 2.9, 3.0, 3.1, 3.2
          if(Math.abs(3.0 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          reviewAverage = "3_0";
          }

          //2.3, 2.4, 2.5, 2.6, 2.7
          if(Math.abs(2.5 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          reviewAverage = "2_5";
          }

          //1.8, 1.9, 2.0, 2.1, 2.2
          if(Math.abs(2.0 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          reviewAverage = "2_0";
          }

          //1.3, 1,4, 1.5, 1.6, 1.7
          if(Math.abs(1.5 - reviewAverage).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          reviewAverage = "1_5";
          }

          // any value < 1.3
          if (reviewAverage < 1.3 && reviewAverage >= 1) {
          reviewAverage = "1_0";
          }

          if (reviewAverage < 1) {
          reviewAverage = "0_0";
          }

          theClassName = "rank" + reviewAverage;
          _reviews += `<div class="c-ReviewsList-item" data-count="${count + 1}">`;

          _reviews += '   <div class="c-Review">';
          _reviews += '     <div class="c-Review-body">';
          _reviews += '       <div class="c-Review-main">';
          _reviews += '         <div class="c-Review-author">';
          _reviews += '           <span>'+review.author_name+'</span>';
          _reviews += '         </div>';
          _reviews += '         <div class="c-Review-date">'+dateDuration+'</div>';
          _reviews += '       </div>';
          _reviews += '       <div class="c-Review-text">';
          _reviews += '         <div class="c-Review-stars">';
          _reviews += '           <span class="c-Review-rating">'+ review.rating_value + ' out of 5</span>';
          _reviews += '           <div class="c-ReviewStars '+theClassName+'">';
          _reviews += `             <span class="sr-only">Rating ${parseFloat(review.rating_value).toFixed}</span>`;
          _reviews += '             <span class="c-ReviewStars-star fa fa-star star1"></span>';
          _reviews += '             <span class="c-ReviewStars-star fa fa-star star2"></span>';
          _reviews += '             <span class="c-ReviewStars-star fa fa-star star3"></span>';
          _reviews += '             <span class="c-ReviewStars-star fa fa-star star4"></span>';
          _reviews += '             <span class="c-ReviewStars-star fa fa-star star5"></span>';
          _reviews += '           </div>';
          _reviews += '         </div>';
          _reviews += '         <div class="c-Review-content">'+review.text+'</div>';
          if (review.review_response) {
            _reviews += 
            `
              <div class="c-Review-comment">
                <div
                  class="c-ReviewComment"
                  <div class="c-ReviewComment-title" >Response from Nicholas</div>
                  <div
                    class="c-ReviewComment-author"
                  </div>
                  <div class="c-ReviewComment-date">${getPastDuration(review.review_response_date)}</div>
                  <div class="c-ReviewComment-content">${review.review_response}</div>
                </div>
              </div>

            `;
          }
          _reviews += '       </div>';
          _reviews += '     </div>';
          _reviews += '   </div>';
          _reviews += '</div>';
        }

        $.each(data.reviews, function(index, review) {
          appendReviews(review, index);
          iLoopCount = index;
          if (index === 20) {
            return false;
          }
        });

        $('.reviewsList').append(_reviews + '</div>');

        let oReviewListSingle = $('.reviewSlideItemWrap > div');
        for (let i = 0; i < oReviewListSingle.length; i += 4) {
            oReviewListSingle.slice(i, i + 4).wrapAll("<div class='reviewSlideItem'>");
        }

        sliderInit();

        function customGetScript(source, callback) {
        var script = document.createElement("script");
        var prior = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
        script.async = 1;

        script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function (_, isAbort) {
          if (isAbort || !script.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test(script.readyState)) {
            script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
            script = undefined;

            if (!isAbort && callback) setTimeout(callback, 0);
          }
        };

        script.src = source;
        prior.parentNode.insertBefore(script, prior);
        }

        function sliderInit() {
        customGetScript(
          "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/slick-carousel/1.8.1/slick.min.js",
          () => {
            $(".reviewSlideItemWrap").slick({
              slidesToShow: 1,
              slidesToScroll: 1,
              speed: 300,
              adaptiveHeight: true,
              variableWidth: false,
              autoplay: false,
              infinite: false,
              dots: false,
              arrows: true,
              prevArrow: $("#reviewPrev"),
              nextArrow: $("#reviewNext"),
              centerMode: true,
              centerPadding: "0",
              cssEase: "ease-in-out",
              draggable: true,
              fade: false,
              focusOnSelect: false,
              pauseOnFocus: true,
              pauseOnDotsHover: false,
              vertical: false,
              verticalSwiping: false,
              rtl: false,
            });

            removeariahidden();
            function removeariahidden() {
                let elementsToGet = document.querySelectorAll(
                  '.slick-slide[aria-hidden="true"]'
                );
                elementsToGet.forEach((item) => {
                  item.removeAttribute("aria-hidden");
                  item.removeAttribute("tabindex");
                });
            }

            $(".reviewSlideItemWrap").on(
              "beforeChange",
              function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
                removeariahidden();
              }
            );

            
            const oReviewsCountWrapper = $('#currentReviewsCount');
            
            function getCurrentSlide(start) {
              let currentSlide = document.querySelector(".slick-current");
              let allSlideItem = currentSlide.querySelectorAll(".c-ReviewsList-item");
              let firstCount = allSlideItem[0].getAttribute("data-count");
              if (parseFloat(firstCount) == 1 && start == true) {
                let lastItem = allSlideItem[allSlideItem.length - 1].getAttribute("data-count");

                    `reviews ${firstCount} - ${lastItem}`
                  );
                }
                
              } else {
                let lastItem = allSlideItem[allSlideItem.length - 1].getAttribute("data-count");
                oReviewsCountWrapper.html(
                  `reviews ${firstCount} - ${lastItem}`
                );
              }
            }

              getCurrentSlide(false);
              removeariahidden();
            });

            getCurrentSlide(true)

  if (widgetKey !== '') {
    $.ajax({
      url: "https://widgets.meetsoci.com/"+widgetKey+"/data.json",
      type: "GET",
      success: function(response) {

          //console.log('response', response)
          
          var _details = processReviewsData(response);

          if (response.summary.rating_value !== 0) {
            //insertAggregateRatingSchema(response.summary.rating_value, response.summary.items_total, response.items)
            addSchemaInsurance(response.summary.rating_value, response.summary.items_total, response.items)
          } else {
            addSchemaInsurance()
          }

          if (_details.reviews.length != 0) {
          //console.log(response);
          //console.log(widgetKey);
          //console.log("_details.reviews.length: " + _details.reviews.length);
          //console.log("_details.average.toFixed(1): " + _details.average.toFixed(1));
          }
      
          document.getElementById("totalReviewsFloating").innerHTML = _details.total ? `${_details.total} `+`${_details.total == 1 ? 'Review' : 'Reviews'}` : `${_details.reviews.length} Review`;
          document.getElementById("totalReviewsContent").innerHTML = _details.total ? `${_details.total} `+`${_details.total == 1 ? 'Review' : 'Reviews'}` : `${_details.reviews.length} Review`;
          
          var test_average = _details.average.toFixed(1);
          
          document.getElementById("averageRatingFloating").innerHTML = test_average + " out of 5"; //testing will remove
          document.getElementById("averageRatingContent").innerHTML = test_average + " out of 5"; //testing will remove
          document.getElementById("averageRatingList").innerHTML = test_average + " out of 5"; //testing will remove
      
          var theClassName = "";
          
          // 4.8, 4.9, 5.0 show 5 full stars
          if(Math.abs(5.0 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){ 
          //do nothing, show 5 stars
          }
          
          //4.3, 4.4, 4.5, 4.6, 4.7 will show the half star at the end
          if(Math.abs(4.5 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2) {
          test_average = "4_5";   
          }

          //3.8, 3.9, 4.0, 4.1, 4.2 show one empty star at the end
          if (Math.abs(4.0 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2) { 
          test_average = "4_0"; 
          }

          //3.3, 3.4, 3.5, 3.6, 3.7 show one empty star at the end and 1 half star before that
          if(Math.abs(3.5 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          test_average = "3_5";
          }

          //2.8, 2.9, 3.0, 3.1, 3.2
          if(Math.abs(3.0 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          test_average = "3_0";
          }

          //2.3, 2.4, 2.5, 2.6, 2.7
          if(Math.abs(2.5 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          test_average = "2_5";
          }

          //1.8, 1.9, 2.0, 2.1, 2.2
          if(Math.abs(2.0 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          test_average = "2_0";
          }

          //1.3, 1,4, 1.5, 1.6, 1.7
          if(Math.abs(1.5 - test_average).toFixed(1) <= 0.2){
          test_average = "1_5";
          }

          // any value < 1.3
          if (test_average < 1.3 && test_average >= 1) {
          test_average = "1_0";
          }

          if (test_average < 1) {
          test_average = "0_0";
          }

          theClassName = "rank" + test_average;
          document.getElementById("c-ReviewStarsFloating").classList.add(theClassName);
          document.getElementById("c-ReviewStarsContent").classList.add(theClassName);
          document.getElementById("c-ReviewStarsList").classList.add(theClassName);
          
          if (_details && _details.reviews.length > 0) {                        
          document.getElementById("totalReviewsFloating").innerHTML = _details.total ? `${_details.total} `+`${_details.total == 1 ? 'Review' : 'Reviews'}` : `${_details.reviews.length} Review`;
          document.getElementById("totalReviewsContent").innerHTML =  _details.total ? `${_details.total} `+`${_details.total == 1 ? 'Review' : 'Reviews'}` : `${_details.reviews.length} Review`;
          document.getElementById("totalReviewsList").innerHTML =  _details.total ? `${_details.total} `+`${_details.total == 1 ? 'review' : 'reviews'}` : `${_details.reviews.length} review`;
              
          if (_details.average.toFixed(1))
              document.getElementById("averageRatingFloating").innerHTML = _details.average.toFixed(1) + " out of 5";
              document.getElementById("averageRatingContent").innerHTML = _details.average.toFixed(1) + " out of 5";

          document.getElementById("reviewSectionFloating").style.display = "block";
          document.getElementById("reviewSectionContent").style.display = "block";
          document.querySelector(".reviews-wrapper").style.display = "block";
          } else {
              document.getElementById("reviewSectionFloating").style.display = "none";
              document.getElementById("reviewSectionContent").style.display = "none";
              document.querySelector(".reviews-wrapper").style.display = "none";
          }
          
          var _details = processReviewsData(response);
          if (_details) {
              populateReviewsHtml(_details);
          }

          if (_details.total == 0 || _details.reviews.length == 0) {
            document.querySelector('.reviews-wrapper').style.display = 'none'
          }
      },
      error: function(error) {
          console.error(error);
      }
  });
  } 
  

</script>

<script>
		var _state = 'TX';
		var _excludedStates = ['CT', 'FL', 'NY'];

		if (_excludedStates.includes(_state)) {

    function getDatesForCurrentWeek() {
	var today = new Date();
	var currentDayOfWeek = today.getDay(); // 0 for Sunday, 1 for Monday, etc.

	const daysUntilMonday = currentDayOfWeek === 0 ? 6 : currentDayOfWeek - 1; // Adjust for Monday as the start of the week
	const startDate = new Date(today);

	const formattedDates = [];

	for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
		const currentDate = new Date(startDate);
		currentDate.setDate(startDate.getDate() + i);

		const _year = currentDate.getFullYear();

		let _month = currentDate.getMonth() + 1;
		const _date = currentDate.getDate();

		const formattedDate = `${_year}-${_month < 10 ? "0" + _month : _month}-${
			_date < 10 ? "0" + _date : _date
		}`;
		formattedDates.push(formattedDate);
	}

	// console.log(formattedDates);
	return formattedDates;
}

// Function to get all special hours
function getSpecialHoursOnDates(daysThisWeek, poi) {
	var _specialHoursTxt = "";
	if (JSON.stringify(poi) === "{}") {
		_specialHoursTxt = "";
	} else {
		_specialHoursTxt = poi.special_hours;
	}

	//console.log("special hours", _specialHoursTxt);

	let _return = {};
	if (_specialHoursTxt) {
		let _specialHoursObj = _specialHoursTxt.split(",");
		let _specialHours = {};

		$.each(_specialHoursObj, function (key, val) {
			var _newVal = val.split(" ");
			var _newKey = _newVal[0].split("-");

			_specialHours[_newKey[2] + "-" + _newKey[0] + "-" + _newKey[1]] = _newVal[1]
				.replace(/:/g, "")
				.split("-");
		});

		$.each(daysThisWeek, function (index, val) {
			if (_specialHours.hasOwnProperty(val)) {
				if (_specialHours[val][0] == "Closed") {
					_return[val] = _specialHours[val][0];
				} else {
					const _open = formatBhoTime(parseFloat(_specialHours[val][0]));
					const _closed = formatBhoTime(parseFloat(_specialHours[val][1]));

					_return[val] = `${_open} - ${_closed}`;
				}
			} else {
				_return[val] = "";
			}
		});
	} else {
		$.each(daysThisWeek, function (index, val) {
			_return[val] = "";
		});
	}

	return _return;
}

function formatBhoTime(time) {
	let theTime;
	if (time === 9999 || time == "9999" || time === "closed" || time === 8799) {
		theTime = "Closed";
	} else if (time < 100) {
		theTime = `12:${time.toString()} AM`;
	} else if (time.toString().length < 4) {
		theTime = `${time.toString().substring(0, 1)}:${time.toString().substring(1, 3)} AM`;
	} else if (time === "1200" || time == 1200) {
		theTime = "12:00 PM";
	} else if (
		time === "1159" ||
		time == 1159 ||
		time === "0000" ||
		time === "2350" ||
		time === 2359
	) {
		theTime = "12:00 AM";
	} else if (time < 1200) {
		theTime = `${time.toString().substring(0, 2)}:${time.toString().substring(2, 4)} AM`;
	} else {
		theTime = `${
			parseInt(time.toString().substring(0, 2) - 12) == 0
				? 12
				: parseInt(time.toString().substring(0, 2) - 12)
		}:${time.toString().substring(2, 4)} PM`;
	}
	return theTime;
}

function getRegularBhoOnDate(dateString, weekIndex, poi) {
	// console.log('dateString', dateString)
	// console.log('weekIndex', weekIndex)
	const dateObject = new Date(dateString);
	let dayOfWeek = 0;

	if (weekIndex == 6) {
		dayOfWeek = 0;
	} else {
		dayOfWeek = weekIndex + 1;
	}
	// console.log(dayOfWeek)

	if (JSON.stringify(poi) === "{}") {
		var temp = "[[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;]]";
	} else {
		var temp = poi.bho;
	}
	if (temp) {
		temp = temp.replace(/&quot;/g, "");
		temp = temp.replace(/0000/g, "1159");
		temp = temp.replace(/\b0+(\d+)\b/g, "$1");
		var dArr = JSON.parse(temp);

		if (dArr.length > 0) {
			var regularHours = dArr[weekIndex];

			if (
				formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == formatBhoTime(regularHours[1]) &&
				formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == "12:00 AM"
			) {
				return `Open 24 Hours`;
			} else if (formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == "Closed") {
				return `Closed`;
			} else {
				return `${formatBhoTime(regularHours[0])} - ${formatBhoTime(regularHours[1])}`;
			}
		} else {
			return "";
		}
	} else {
		return "";
	}
}

function formatTimeRange(openingTime, closingTime) {
	return `${openingTime} - ${closingTime}`;
}

function formatResult(inputObj) {
	// const daysInWeek = ["Monday", "Tuesday", "Wednesday", "Thursday", "Friday", "Saturday", "Sunday"];
	const daysInWeek = [
		"Sunday",
		"Monday",
		"Tuesday",
		"Wednesday",
		"Thursday",
		"Friday",
		"Saturday",
	];
	const hoursArr = Object.entries(inputObj);
	let resultArr = [];
	let resultHtml = "";

	// console.log(hoursArr);
	// console.log(daysInWeek);


	let i = 0;
	$.each(hoursArr, function (index, value) {

		const dateString = value[0];
		const parts = dateString.split('-');
		const year = parseInt(parts[0], 10);
		const month = parseInt(parts[1], 10) - 1; 
		const day = parseInt(parts[2], 10);

		//console.log('dateString', dateString)

		var _dayDate = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month, day, 12, 0, 0));

		//console.log('_dayDate', _dayDate)

		if (i > 0) {
			resultHtml += `<tr class="hoursRow hoursRow${[
				index,
			]} hoursRowClosed c-hours-details-row js-day-of-week-row">
			<td class="hoursDay c-hours-details-row-day">${daysInWeek[_dayDate.getDay()]}</td>
			<td class="hoursTime hours${
				daysInWeek[_dayDate.getDay()]
			}"><span class="c-hours-details-row-intervals-instance js-hours-interval-instance">${
				value[1]
			}</span></td>
		</tr>`;
		} else {
			resultHtml += `
			<tr id="hoursToday" class="hoursRow hoursRowActive hoursRow${[
				index,
			]} hoursRowClosed c-hours-details-row js-day-of-week-row is-today">
				<td class="hoursDay c-hours-details-row-day">Today</td>
				<td id="todayHours" class="hoursTime hours${
					daysInWeek[_dayDate.getDay()]
				}"><span class="c-hours-details-row-intervals-instance js-hours-interval-instance">${
				value[1]
			}</span></td>
			</tr>
			`;
		}

		i++;
	});


	return resultHtml;
}

function getTodayHours() {
	// Get Date and Day Index Today
	const today = new Date();
	const dayOfWeek = today.getDay();

	var temp = "[[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;0830&quot;,&quot;0530&quot;],[&quot;9999&quot;,&quot;9999&quot;]]";
	if (temp) {
		temp = temp.replace(/&quot;/g, "");
		temp = temp.replace(/0000/g, "1159");
		temp = temp.replace(/\b0+(\d+)\b/g, "$1");
		var dArr = JSON.parse(temp);

		if (dArr.length > 0) {
			var regularHours = dArr[dayOfWeek];

			if (
				formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == formatBhoTime(regularHours[1]) &&
				formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == "12:00 AM"
			) {
				return `Open 24 Hours`;
			} else if (formatBhoTime(regularHours[0]) == "Closed") {
				return `Closed`;
			} else {
				return `${formatBhoTime(regularHours[0])} - ${formatBhoTime(regularHours[1])}`;
			}
		} else {
			return "";
		}
	} else {
		return "";
	}
}

// Function to populate regular or store hours per day this week
function populateHoursForDays() {
	// Call the function to get the formatted dates for the current week starting on Monday.
	const daysThisWeek = getDatesForCurrentWeek();
	//console.log(daysThisWeek)

	// Populate special hours first
	const businessHours = getSpecialHoursOnDates(daysThisWeek, {});

	// console.log(businessHours)
	// Among the special hours, check which ones don't have a value and use bho for those
	// let index = 0;
	$.each(businessHours, function (date, hours) {
		if (hours == "") {
			const dateString = date;
			const parts = dateString.split('-');
			const year = parseInt(parts[0], 10);
			const month = parseInt(parts[1], 10) - 1; 
			const day = parseInt(parts[2], 10);


			var d = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month, day, 12, 0, 0));
			let index = d.getDay();
			businessHours[date] = getRegularBhoOnDate(date, index, {});
		}
		// index++;
	});

	// Get Date Today
	const today = new Date();
	const _todayYear = today.getFullYear();
	const _todayDate = today.getDate();
	let _todayMonth = today.getMonth() + 1;
	const formattedDate = `${_todayYear}-${_todayMonth < 10 ? "0" + _todayMonth : _todayMonth}-${
		_todayDate < 10 ? "0" + _todayDate : _todayDate
	}`;

	//console.log(formattedDate);
	//console.log(businessHours[formattedDate]);
	// console.log(businessHours);

	$("#storeHours").html(formatResult(businessHours));
	checkTodaySchedNew(businessHours, daysThisWeek);
}


let bhoData = {
	bho: [["9999","9999"],["0830","0530"],["0830","0530"],["0830","0530"],["0830","0530"],["0830","0530"],["9999","9999"]]
}

if (bhoData.bho.length > 0) {
	populateHoursForDays();
	addFAQhours();
	$('.Core-hours').css('display', 'block')
	$('.Hero-hours').css('display', 'block')
	$('.FAQ-listItem[data-type="hours"]').css('display', 'block')
} else {
	$('.Core-hours').css('display', 'none')
	$('.Hero-hours').css('display', 'none')
	$('.FAQ-listItem[data-type="hours"]').css('display', 'none')
}


function checkTodaySchedNew(data, days) {
	const oHoursWrapper = $("#hoursDataDays");
	const daysInWeek = [
		"Sunday",
		"Monday",
		"Tuesday",
		"Wednesday",
		"Thursday",
		"Friday",
		"Saturday",
	];

	let _return = "";

	init(0);

	function init(currentIndex) {
		let dataToUse = data[days[currentIndex]];
		if (dataToUse != "Closed" && dataToUse != "Open 24 Hours") {
			let timeArr = data[days[currentIndex]].split(" - ");
			let openTime = convertTo24hrformat(timeArr[0]);
			let closeTime = convertTo24hrformat(timeArr[1]);
			let currentTime = convertTo24hrformat(formatAMPM(new Date()));
			if (currentTime < openTime && currentTime < closeTime) {
				oHoursWrapper.html(`Closed &#x2022; Opens at ${timeArr[0]}`);
				return;
			}
			if (currentTime > openTime && currentTime < closeTime) {
				oHoursWrapper.html(`Open Now &#x2022; Closes at ${timeArr[1]}`);
				return;
			}
			if (currentTime > openTime && currentTime > closeTime) {
				checkOtherdayIfOpen(currentIndex + 1);
				return;
			}
		} else if (dataToUse == "Open 24 Hours") {
			oHoursWrapper.html(`Opens 24 Hours`);
			return;
		} else {
			// init(currentIndex + 1)
			checkOtherdayIfOpen(currentIndex + 1);
		}
	}

	function checkOtherdayIfOpen(currentIndex) {
		if (currentIndex < 7) {
			let dataToUse = data[days[currentIndex]];

			const dateString = days[currentIndex];
			const parts = dateString.split('-');
			const year = parseInt(parts[0], 10);
			const month = parseInt(parts[1], 10) - 1; 
			const day = parseInt(parts[2], 10);


			var d = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month, day, 12, 0, 0));
			let ctr = d.getDay();

			if (dataToUse != "Closed" && dataToUse != "Open 24 Hours") {
				let timeArr = data[days[currentIndex]].split(" - ");
				let openTime = convertTo24hrformat(timeArr[0]);
				oHoursWrapper.html(`Closed &#x2022; Opens at ${timeArr[0]} ${daysInWeek[ctr]}`);
			} else if (dataToUse == "Open 24 Hours") {
				oHoursWrapper.html(`Closed &#x2022; Opens at 12:00 AM ${daysInWeek[ctr]}`);
				return;
			} else {
				checkOtherdayIfOpen(currentIndex + 1);
			}
		}
	}

	function formatAMPM(date) {
		var hours = date.getHours();
		var minutes = date.getMinutes();
		var ampm = hours >= 12 ? "PM" : "AM";
		hours = hours % 12;
		hours = hours ? hours : 12; // the hour '0' should be '12'
		minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
		var strTime = hours + ":" + minutes + " " + ampm;
		return strTime;
	}

	function convertTo24hrformat(time) {
		var hours = Number(time.match(/^(\d+)/)[1]);
		var minutes = Number(time.match(/:(\d+)/)[1]);
		var AMPM = time.match(/\s(.*)$/)[1];
		if (AMPM == "PM" && hours < 12) hours = hours + 12;
		if (AMPM == "AM" && hours == 12) hours = hours - 12;
		var sHours = hours.toString();
		var sMinutes = minutes.toString();
		if (hours < 10) sHours = "0" + sHours;
		if (minutes < 10) sMinutes = "0" + sMinutes;

		return sHours + sMinutes;
	}
}

function addFAQhours() {
	let _returnHTML = "";
	let data = [
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Monday",
			opens: "08:30",
			closes: "05:30",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Tuesday",
			opens: "08:30",
			closes: "05:30",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Wednesday",
			opens: "08:30",
			closes: "05:30",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Thursday",
			opens: "08:30",
			closes: "05:30",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Friday",
			opens: "08:30",
			closes: "05:30",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Saturday",
			opens: "CLOSED",
			closes: "CLOSED",
		},
		{
			dayOfWeek: "Sunday",
			opens: "CLOSED",
			closes: "CLOSED",
		},
	];

	data.forEach((item) => {
		if (item.opens == "00:00" && item.closes == "23:59") {
			_returnHTML += `
				<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>Open 24 Hours</span><br />
			`;
		} else if (item.opens == "00:00" && item.closes == "00:00") {
			_returnHTML += `
				<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>Open 24 Hours</span><br />
			`;
		} else if (item.opens == "23:59" && item.closes == "00:00") {
			_returnHTML += `
				<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>Open 24 Hours</span><br />
			`;
		} else if (item.opens == "23:59" && item.closes == "23:59") {
			_returnHTML += `
				<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>Open 24 Hours</span><br />
			`;
		} else if (item.opens === "CLOSED") {
			_returnHTML += `
			<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>Closed</span><br />
		`;
		} else if (item.opens !== "CLOSED") {
			_returnHTML += `
			<span class="faq-days-textdata">${item.dayOfWeek}:</span> <span>${convertToAMPM(
				item.opens
			)} - ${convertToAMPM(item.closes)}</span><br />
		`;
		}
	});

	_returnHTML += `
			Night &amp; Weekends by appointment
		`;

	$("#FAQHours").html(_returnHTML);

	function convertToAMPM(timeStr) {
		let [hours, minutes] = timeStr.split(":").map(Number);
		let period = hours < 12 ? "AM" : "PM";
		hours = hours % 12 || 12;
		return `${parseFloat(hours.toString().padStart(2, "0"))}:${minutes
			.toString()
			.padStart(2, "0")} ${period}`;
	}
}




</script>

</html>
